 paanch saal tak krantikari dal kaa vidhayak suresh nazar nahin aata he, badlaav dal kaa ramesh har mudde par awaz uthaata he

 naaraaz ramesh badlaav dal chodta he or krantikari dal kaa daaman tham letaa he
 Now you have two situations in front of the aware voter
 jis party ko aap vot nahin dena chaahate the vahaan se ab aapkaa pasandida netaa khadaa he
 The party you want to vote from is the candidate you want to defeat
 aap bataaiye aap vot kise denge
 Will choose the right party or the right candidate
 sahi party chunane ke liye aapako badlaav dal ko vot karnaa hoga, sahi ummidavaar chunane ke liye aapako krantikari dal ko vot karnaa hoga
 i leave the answer to you
 yah jaanate hue ki matdaan karnaa aasaan faisla nahin hota he
 Is it not strange that you have no sympathy for the workers who work day and night for the party you want to win? aap duusare dal se aae ummidavaar ko vot kar dete hai
 Each team has a defection branch
 dal or dalbadalu donon hi maukaparast hote hai
 It is also true that the issue of defection and familism dominates for only two-three days of ticket distribution
 uske baad reliyaan shuru hote hi sara manzar kuch or ho jaataa he
 The issue of defection and familism ends
 phir agle chunaav main ubharta he
 There are five assembly seats in Ghaziabad district
 yahaan bhaajapa ne ek dalbadalu ko tikat diya he
 The Congress has also given ticket to a defector
 basapa ne kisi dalbadalu ko tikat nahin diya he
 Hapur district has three assembly seats
 basapa ne kisi dalbadalu ko tikat nahin diya he
 The SP has also not given any defectors
 bijepi ne ek dalbadalu ko tikat diya he
 Former MP Ramesh Chandra Tomar who was given a ticket from Noida Lok Sabha by Congress in 2014
 tomars ne ain vakt par chunaav ladane se manaa kar diya or bijepi main shaamil ho gaye
 Has been a BJP MP four times
 2009 main congress ke tikat par loksabhaa chunaav lard chuke hai
 There are 12 assembly seats in Allahabad
 basapa ne ek dalbadalu ko tikat diya he
 The BJP has announced 8 names, of which 5 are defectors
 sapa or congress ne ek bhi dalbadalu ko tikat nahin diya he
 There are seven assembly seats in Buldanshar district
 yahaan se bhaajapa, basapa ne ek-ek dalbadalu ko tikat diya he
 The Rashtriya Lok Dal has given tickets to five defectors
 ralod ke tikat par sapa or bhaajapa se aae netaa chunaav lard rahe hai
 Banaras district has eight seats
 bhaajapa, sapa or congress ne yahaan aadhikarik rup se naam kii ghoshnaa nahin kii he
 The BSP has not given tickets to any defectors
 naamon kii ghoshnaa kar di he
 Ballia has seven assembly seats
 basapa ne abhi tak ek dalbadalu ko tikat diya he
 The SP has announced the names on 6 seats but has not given tickets to any defectors
 bhaajapa ne ek hi seat kii ghoshnaa kii he, dalbadalu ko nahin diya he
 The ruckus seems to indicate that all parties have ignored the original workers and given tickets to the outsiders
 magar zilaavaar jaakar dekhne se lagata he ki dalbadalu to sabake yahaan hai
 There is less in some district or more in some
 'dainik bhaskar' ne likhaa he ki bhaajapa ne abhi tak 300 ummidavaaron main se 30 dalbadaluon ko tikat diya he
 Another issue is familism
 is baar bijepi main kai pariwaron ko tikat mila to congress, sapa or basapa ke bheetar ke parivaarwaad public kii nazar se batch gaye
 The BJP certainly opposes dynasticism, but now its leaders are differentiating from Gandhian familyism and dynasticism of their father-sons politics
 congress ke randeep surajevaala ne jawaab nahin diya
 He is himself the son of a politician
 bijepi ke om maathur ne jawaab diya ki wo gandhiparivaar ke vanshavaad or bhaajapa ke bheetar ke nae nae pariwaron main fark karte hai
 What he means is that the Gandhi family in the Congress only sits on the upper chair
 bijepi main parivaar ke sadsy ko kaaryakarta se upar kii ore chadhana padataa he
 Have to work in the organization
 hamane kuch din pehle upi bijepi ke bheetar parivaarwaad kii ginati kii thi
 Many names have been added to it
 bijepi ke bheetar kalyaan parivaar sapa parivaar kaa muqabla karata lag rahaa he
 Kalyan Singh is the Governor
 unke bete bijepi se saansad hai
 Son's son got assembly ticket
 bahu ko bhi tikat mila he
 The Rajnath family has come into the race with Pankaj Singh getting the ticket
 saansadon or netaaon kii patniyon, beton or bahu ke naam ke aadhaar par bhaajapa ke bheetar ke pariwaron ke naam is prakaar hai brijabhooshan parivaar, sarvesh parivaar, kaushal kishor parivaar, maury parivaar, tandon parivaar, hukum parivaar, raahi parivaar, katiyaar parivaar, shastri parivaar, vaajapeyi parivaar, treepathi parivaar, gangavar parivaar, chulbul singh parivaar, shrivastav parivaar, raay parivaar, kapur parivaar
 This does not mean that familyism has stopped in BSP, Congress and SP
 upi main mulaayam singh kunbe kaa koi parivaar muqabla nahin kar saktaa he
 The list of Mulayam Singh Yadav's clan is becoming so long that one day UP will get four teams from this family
 is chunaav main bhi yadav parivaar ke do nae sanskaran launch hue hai
 Ramgopal Yadav's nephew Arvind Singh Yadav has got the ticket from Chibramau seat of Kannauj
 pheraari car vaale pratik yadav kii patni aparnaa yadav ko lakhanu kaint se tikat mila he
 Apart from this, SP has many families like Azam family, Agarwal family, Ansari family
 congress ne punjab main kai tikat parivaarwaad ke aadhaar par baante hai
 Rather, Captain Amarinder Singh, in view of the demand for tickets in the name of familism, drew a unique rule of 'one family one ticket'
 media report ke aadhaar par congress ne parivaarwaad ke aadhaar par 13 tikat diye hai
 Every party has given tickets on the basis of familyism, but the credit for such quota should go to Captain Saheb
 goa or upi ke liye congress ne aisa niyam nahin banaaya he
 In Goa, the Congress has given the father-son ticket
 pati-patni ko tikat diya he
 BSP has also got tickets on the basis of familyism
 tippaniyan Now the voter has to decide whether to elect a government or a candidate in the election
 ummidavaar chunate vakt dal-badal, parivaarwaad kaa bhi ilaaj kare
 Although the job of a voter is to choose a candidate, it is not his job to choose a government
 aap matadaata hi bataa sakenge ki raajnneeti or raajnneetik dal ke bheetar pratibhaaon ko koun zyaada roak rahaa he
 Money or Familyism
